{{Top|real|can}}
{{Youmay|listing [[canon]] media by [[in-universe]] chronology|[[Wookieepedia]]'s [[timeline of galactic history]], which lists canon events by chronological order|linebreak=1}}
{{Overhaul}}
{{Citation}}
This '''timeline''' is intended to list narrative-based [[canon]] media by an [[in-universe]] chronology. The list includes films, television episodes, novels, [[Star Wars comic books|comic books]], short stories, [[video game]]s, and other promotional material.

There are several defined criteria considered when including ''Star Wars'' canon media on this timeline:
*Media must have a direct narrative story that is told in-universe. This dictates that [[:Category:Canon reference books|reference books]], visual guides, and [[:Category:Art books|art books]] are not included in this list, and neither are in-universe media with no narrative, such as [[:Category:Replica journals|replica journals]].
*All media, except for the original and prequel films and the ''Star Wars: The Clone Wars'' [[Star Wars: The Clone Wars (film)|film]] and [[Star Wars: The Clone Wars|TV series]], must have been released after [[April 25]], [[2014]], when Disney relaunched the official ''Star Wars'' canon.<ref name="Legends">{{SW|url=news/the-legendary-star-wars-expanded-universe-turns-a-new-page|text=The Legendary Star Wars Expanded Universe Turns a New Page}}</ref>
*All adaptations and novelizations since the relaunch are considered canon, though this status will be noted alongside entry titles. Novelizations of canon films released prior to the canon relaunch are, however, not canon.
*Books that fill all above criteria are listed regardless of intended age range, but the timeline does distinguish between Novels, Junior Novels, and Young Readers books. All Novels are published by [[Del Rey]] Books, [[Random House Worlds]], [[Egmont UK Ltd]], or [[Disney–Lucasfilm Press]], the latter of which also publishes most Junior Novels and Young Readers books.
*Categorisation of books as either Junior Novels or Young Readers is based on age ranges provided by Disney Publishing Worldwide's online catalogue, however, these age ranges can be inconsistent and unreliable.
*All video games are considered canon regardless of platform or gameplay.

This timeline allows for sorting and filtering by various details including media format and in-universe dates following the [[galactic standard calendar]] (BBY/ABY). In-universe or publication eras such as [[Imperial Era]] have not been included due to inconsistent use by Lucasfilm.

Placement of media in the timeline observes [[in-universe]] chronology. In order to ensure reliability, sources must ''always'' be included when providing dates. The order of chronology within the timeline adheres to the following criteria:
*All entries are ordered based on the beginning of the "main events", as defined in the [[Wookieepedia:Layout_Guide#Appearances|Layout Guide]].
*Official sources for timeline placements are always given precedent over "logical" placements.
*The order in which full adaptations are listed are as follows: '''Film, Novel, Junior Novel, Young Readers, Graphic Novel, Comic Book Miniseries'''.
*Short story anthologies are broken down into individual titles and placed according to story-specific dates. However, anthologies with consistently connecting narration throughout the stories are treated as one entry.

† - Exact placement currently unknown.

As the battle is dated to [[20 BBY]] by ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]'', the short story must take place around 20 or 19 [['ABY-BBY' dating system|BBY]].</ref> ||style="background-color: #C6D9F0; text-align: center;" | SS ||"[[Bug (short story)|Bug]]" †

|data-sort-value=-18 |c. [[17 BBY]]<ref name="RescueDate">''[[Star Wars: Timelines]]'' states that [[Wilhuff Tarkin]] was assigned to [[Sentinel Base]] in [[17 BBY]]. Since ''Adventures in Wild Space: The Rescue'' features Tarkin in command of Sentinel Base, ''The Rescue'' must be set during or after 17 [['ABY-BBY' dating system|BBY]]. Additionally, ''The Rescue'' takes place shortly after ''[[Adventures in Wild Space: The Steal]]'', which ''[[Star Wars: Timelines]]'' dates to [[18 BBY]], placing ''The Rescue'' around 17 BBY.</ref> ||style="background-color: #FAC08F; text-align: center;" | JR ||''[[Adventures in Wild Space: The Rescue]]''

|data-sort-value=-14 |[[14 BBY]]<ref name="DV18 date">{{DVDLotS18}}</ref> ||style="background-color: #CCC1D9; text-align: center;" | C ||[[Darth Vader (2017) 18|''Darth Vader'' (2017) 18]]
||[[Charles Soule]]
|| 2018-07-11
|- class="comic"
|[[14 BBY]]<ref name="DV 19/20/21/22">The events of [[Tarkin (novel)|''Tarkin'']] take place five [[Standard year|years]] after the [[Proclamation of the New Order|rise]] of the [[Galactic Empire]], which ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]'' dates to [[19 BBY]]. Therefore, ''Tarkin'' must be set in [[14 BBY]]. As [[Anakin Skywalker|Darth Vader]] knows about [[Wilhuff Tarkin]]'s past on [[Eriadu]] in [[Darth Vader (2017) 18|''Darth Vader'' (2017) 18]], which he only learned about in ''Tarkin'', issue 18 must take place after the novel. The later issue [[Darth Vader (2017) 19|''Darth Vader'' (2017) 19]] featured the [[Second Sister]], who was [[Death|killed]] in ''[[Star Wars Jedi: Fallen Order]]''. ''Fallen Order'' takes place five years after the [[Great Jedi Purge]], which is dated to 19 BBY by ''Star Wars: Galactic Atlas''. Therefore, ''Star Wars Jedi: Fallen Order'' is also set in 14 BBY. As ''Darth Vader: Dark Lord of the Sith 19'' is set immediately after issue 18, and issues 20, 21 and 22 all take place after each other, it means that all these issues take place in [[14 BBY]].</ref> ||style="background-color: #CCC1D9; text-align: center;" | C ||[[Darth Vader (2017) 19|''Darth Vader'' (2017) 19]]
||[[Charles Soule]]
|| 2018-08-08

||[[Charles Soule]]

|data-sort-value=-10 |[[10 BBY]]<ref name="Timelines" /> ||style="background-color: #92CDDC; text-align: center;" | F ||''[[Solo: A Star Wars Story]]''
*<small>Prologue occurs in [[13 BBY]].<ref name="Solo prologue">''[[Solo: A Star Wars Story The Official Guide]]'' establishes that the events of ''Solo: A Star Wars Story'' begin nine [[Standard year|years]] after the [[Proclamation of the New Order|founding]] of the [[Galactic Empire]]. ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]'' dates the Empire's founding to [[19 BBY]], meaning the events of ''Solo'' can be placed in [[10 BBY]]. Because the prologue takes place three years prior, the prologue must take place in [[13 BBY]].</ref></small>

|- class="tv"
|c. [[4 BBY|4]]&ndash;[[3 BBY]]<ref name="DisarmingLesson">"A Disarming Lesson" takes place after [[Ezra Bridger]] meets [[Ahsoka Tano]] in "[[Fire Across the Galaxy]]," but before [[Ezra Bridger's lightsaber|his lightsaber]] is destroyed in "[[Twilight of the Apprentice]]." ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]'' places "Fire Across the Galaxy" in [[4 BBY]], and according to ''[[Star Wars: Absolutely Everything You Need to Know, Updated and Expanded]]'', [[Ahsoka Tano]] was 14 [[Standard year|years]] old when [[Gender|she]] became [[Anakin Skywalker]]'s [[Padawan]] and 32 when she fought him as Darth Vader in "Twilight of the Apprentice." ''Star Wars: Galactic Atlas'' states that Tano was apprenticed to Skywalker in [[22 BBY]], meaning "Twilight of the Apprentice" cannot be set any later than [[3 BBY]]. ''[[Dawn of Rebellion]]'' places "[[The Mystery of Chopper Base]]" in 3 [['ABY-BBY' dating system|BBY]], and since "Twilight of the Apprentice" takes place after that episode, it must be set in 3 BBY. Therefore, "A Disarming Lesson" takes place between 4 BBY and 3 BBY.</ref> ||style="background-color: #B7DDE8; text-align: center;" | TV ||[[A Disarming Lesson|''Forces of Destiny'': Season 2: Episode 15: "A Disarming Lesson"]] †
||[[Nicole Dubuc]]

|data-sort-value=-4 |Between [[4 BBY]] and [[3 BBY]]<ref name="Heist">''[[Star Wars Rebels: Imperial Heist]]'' includes [[Sabine Wren]] with [[Color|blue-green]] [[hair]], which first appears in "[[The Lost Commanders]]," however it takes place before [[Kanan Jarrus]] was blinded in "[[Twilight of the Apprentice]]." ''[[Star Wars: The Clone Wars: Character Encyclopedia - Join the Battle!]]'' states that [[Rex]] was [[Reproduction|born]] thirty-two [[Standard year|years]] before the events of [[Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope|''Star Wars'': Episode IV ''A New Hope'']], which ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]'' places in [[0 BBY]]. Therefore, Rex must have been born in [[32 BBY]]. As it also states that Rex is 28 during "The Lost Commanders", this episode must take place in [[4 BBY]]. As {{SW|url=news/swca-2022-lucasfilm-publishing-behind-the-page-panel|text=SWCC 2022: 7 Things We Learned from the Lucasfilm Publishing Behind the Page Panel}}, dates "Twilight of the Apprentice" to [[3 BBY]], ''Star Wars Rebels: Imperial Heist'' must take place between these years.</ref> ||style="background-color: #C3D69B; text-align: center;" | VG ||''[[Star Wars Rebels: Imperial Heist]]'' †

Additionally, Sabine's hair is light-purple in ''[[Star Wars Rebels: Steps Into Shadow]]'', meaning "The Second Chance" must take place some time prior. |data-sort-value=-2 |[[2 BBY]]<ref name="Timelines" /> ||style="background-color: #B7DDE8; text-align: center;" | TV ||[[Imperial Supercommandos|''Star Wars Rebels'': Season 3: Episode 7: "Imperial Super Commandos"]]

|| 2016-11-05
|- class="videogame"
|data-sort-value=-2 |c. [[2 BBY]]&ndash;[[1 BBY]]<ref name="Special Ops">''Special Ops'' features [[Sabine Wren]] with light [[Color|purple]] [[hair]] and a [[jetpack]], placing it after the events of ''[[Imperial Supercommandos]]'', where she obtains the jetpack, and before "[[The Occupation]]", where her hair is deep purple. ''[[Dawn of Rebellion]]'' dates the events of ''[[Star Wars Rebels: Steps Into Shadow]]'' seventeen [[Standard year|years]] after the end of the [[Clone Wars]], which ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]'' dates to [[19 BBY]]; therefore, the events of ''Steps Into Shadow'' must take place in [[2 BBY]] and ''Imperial Supercommandos'', which comes after, can be set no earlier than [[2 BBY]]. Because Sabine Wren's hair is deep purple in "[[The Occupation]]", ''Special Ops'' must take place prior to that episode. The trivia guide for ''[[Star Wars Rebels: Heroes of Mandalore]]'' states that [[Bo-Katan Kryze]] was redesigned to advance the character's age by "18 [[Standard year|years]] or so". As she was last seen was in "[[The Lawless]]," which ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]'' places in [[19 BBY]], it can be assumed that the events of ''Heroes of Mandalore'', as well as ''The Occupation'' take place in approximately 1 BBY. Because Special Ops must be set between these episodes, this information places it between 2 BBY and 1 BBY.</ref> ||style="background-color: #C3D69B; text-align: center;" | VG ||''[[Star Wars Rebels: Special Ops]]'' †

|c. [[3 BBY|3]]&ndash;[[0 BBY]]<ref name="Beast Within">"The Beast Within" features [[Ezra's second lightsaber]], which was constructed after the events of "[[Twilight of the Apprentice]]." According to {{SW|url=news/swca-2022-lucasfilm-publishing-behind-the-page-panel|text=SWCC 2022: 7 Things We Learned from the Lucasfilm Publishing Behind the Page Panel}}, "Twilight of the Apprentice" takes place in [[3 BBY]]. Furthermore, [[Ezra Bridger]] disappears during the events of "[[Family Reunion – and Farewell]]," and according to ''[[The Star Wars Book]]'' "Family Reunion – and Farewell" takes place in the same [[Standard year|year]] as the [[Battle of Yavin]], or [[0 BBY]]. Therefore, "The Beast Within" takes place some time between 3 [['ABY-BBY' dating system|BBY]] and 0 BBY.</ref>||style="background-color: #CCC1D9; text-align: center;" | C ||"[[The Beast Within]]" †
|[[Alec Worley]]

|- class="short"
|data-sort-value=0 |Between [[2 BBY]] and [[0 BBY]]<ref name="Inbrief Date">''[[Star Wars: On the Front Lines]]'' places the [[Declaration of the Rebel Alliance]] two [[Standard year|years]] before the [[Battle of Yavin]], or [[2 BBY]]. As the Rebel Alliance appears in "Inbrief," it must therefore have taken place during or after 2 [['ABY-BBY' dating system|BBY]]. Furthermore, in ''[[Battlefront: Twilight Company]]'', the [[rebel trooper]] [[Hazram Namir]] refers to [[Brand]] as a [[bounty hunter]] during the [[battle on Vir Aphshire]], which occurs concurrently with the [[Battle of Yavin]]. As Brand's [[bounty]] [[Hunting|hunter]] past was not known by other rebels until the events of "Inbrief", it must take place prior to the Battle of [[Yavin Prime|Yavin]], or [[0 BBY]]. Therefore "Inbrief" takes place in between 2 BBY and 0 BBY.</ref> ||style="background-color: #C6D9F0; text-align: center;" | SS ||"[[Inbrief]]" †
||[[Janine K. Spendlove]]
|| 2015-11-10
|- class="short"
||Between [[2 BBY]] and [[4 ABY]]<ref name="Kindling">"The Kindling" features the [[Alliance to Restore the Republic|Rebel Alliance]], which formed two [[Standard year|years]] before the [[Battle of Yavin]] according to ''[[Star Wars: On the Front Lines]]'', and became the [[New Republic]] in [[4 ABY]] according to ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]''. As ''Star Wars: Galactic Atlas'' also dates the Battle of Yavin to [[0 BBY]], the Rebel Alliance must have been founded in [[2 BBY]] and "The Kindling" takes place some time between these years.</ref> ||style="background-color: #C6D9F0; text-align: center;" | SS ||[[The Kindling]] †
||[[Cavan Scott]]<br />[[George Mann]]

| c. [[2 BBY|2]]&ndash;[[0 BBY]]<ref name="DarkVisions">''[[Star Wars: Vader - Dark Visions]]'' takes place after the formation of the [[Alliance to Restore the Republic|Rebel Alliance]], as it appears in the [[Vader - Dark Visions 2|previous]] and [[Vader - Dark Visions 4|following]] issues, but prior to the destruction of the [[DS-1 Death Star Mobile Battle Station|Death Star]], as it appears in this issue. ''[[Star Wars: On the Front Lines]]'' dates the formation of the Rebel Alliance to [[2 BBY]], and ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]'' dates the destruction of the Death Star to [[0 BBY]], meaning that ''Star Wars: Vader - Dark Visions'' takes place some time prior.</ref>||style="background-color: #CCC1D9; text-align: center;" | C ||[[Vader - Dark Visions 2|''Vader - Dark Visions'' 2]] †

|- class="comic"
|[[0 BBY]]<ref name="Obi-Wan mini">{{SW|url=news/marvel-star-wars-may-2022-exclusive-preview|text=A Tale from Obi-Wan's Youngling Days and More from Marvel's May 2022 ''Star Wars'' Comics &ndash; Exclusive Preview}} establishes that ''Obi-Wan'' 1 takes place during [[Obi-Wan Kenobi]]'s final [[Standard day|days]] on [[Tatooine]], and since [[Gender|him]] leaving Tatooine and his [[death]] in [[Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope|''Star Wars'': Episode IV ''A New Hope'']] are dated to [[0 BBY]] in ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]'', ''Obi-Wan'' 1 must take place around the same [[Standard year|year]].</ref> ||style="background-color: #CCC1D9; text-align: center;" | C ||[[Obi-Wan 1|''Obi-Wan'' 1]] †
*<small>Flashbacks occur in [[49 BBY]].</small><ref name="Obi-Wan 1 flashback">The flashbacks in [[Obi-Wan 1|''Obi-Wan'' 1]] take place when [[Obi-Wan Kenobi]] is eight [[Standard year|years]] old, and since {{SWCT|Obi-Wan Kenobi - Padawan - Base Series 1|Obi-Wan Kenobi - Padawan - ''Base Series 1''}} establishes that he was born 57 years before ''Star Wars'': Episode IV ''A New Hope'', which corresponds to [[57 BBY]], he was eight years old in [[49 BBY]].</ref>
||[[Christopher Cantwell]]
|| 2022-05-04
|- class="comic"
|[[0 BBY]]<ref name="Obi-Wan mini" /> ||style="background-color: #CCC1D9; text-align: center;" | C ||[[Obi-Wan 2|''Obi-Wan'' 2]] †
* <small>Flashbacks occur between [[44 BBY|44]]-[[32 BBY]].</small><ref name="Obi-Wan 2 flashback">In the [[Obi-Wan 2|''Obi-Wan'' 2]] flashbacks, [[Obi-Wan Kenobi]] is [[Qui-Gon Jinn]]'s [[padawan]]. ''[[Master & Apprentice]]'' establishes that Kenobi became Jinn's padawan when he was thirteen [[Standard year|years]] old. Since [[Star Wars: Card Trader|''Star Wars'': Card Trader]] states he was [[Reproduction|born]] 57 years before the [[Battle of Yavin]]&mdash;[[0 BBY]] according to ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]'' &mdash;Kenobi became Jinn's padawan in [[44 BBY]]. He remained so until Jinn's [[death]], which occurred in [[32 BBY]] according to ''Galactic Atlas''.</ref>
||[[Christopher Cantwell]]
|| 2022-06-29
|- class="comic"
|[[0 BBY]]<ref name="Obi-Wan mini" /> ||style="background-color: #CCC1D9; text-align: center;" | C ||[[Obi-Wan 3|''Obi-Wan'' 3]] †
*<small>Flashbacks occur in [[22 BBY]].</small><ref name="Obi-Wan 3 flashback">The [[Obi-Wan 3|''Obi-Wan'' 3]] flashbacks take place shortly after the [[Defense of Rishi Station]], which appears in "[[Rookies]]." {{TCWcanondates|105}} Therefore ''Obi-Wan'' 3 also takes place around 22 [['ABY-BBY' dating system|BBY]].</ref>
||[[Christopher Cantwell]]

*<small>Flashbacks occur between [[20 BBY|20]]-[[19 BBY]].</small><ref name="Obi-Wan 4 flashback">The flashbacks of [[Obi-Wan 4|''Obi-Wan'' 4]] take place after the [[Devaron massacre]] from "[[Monster]]," which ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]'' dates to [[20 BBY]], and before the end of the [[Clone Wars]], which ''Star Wars: Galactic Atlas'' also dates to [[19 BBY]].</ref>

| [[0 ABY|0]]&ndash;[[4 ABY]]<ref name="Commander Dating">''[[Star Wars: Timelines]]'' dates the start of ''[[Star Wars: Commander]]'' to [[0 ABY]], between the events of ''[[The Weapon of a Jedi: A Luke Skywalker Adventure]]'' and [[Star Wars (2015) 1|''Star Wars'' (2015) 1]].. Furthermore, the game features [[Anakin Skywalker|Darth Vader]] and [[Bib Fortuna]], who both die in [[4 ABY]], meaning that Commander must be set in between these two dates, placing it some time between 0 ABY and 4 ABY.</ref> ||style="background-color: #C3D69B; text-align: center;" | VG ||''[[Star Wars: Commander]]''

|| 2020-10-14
|- class="videogame"
|data-sort-value=5 |[[5 ABY]]<ref name="B2-5ABY">''[[Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary]]'' dates [[Han Solo]] meeting with an [[Galactic Empire|Imperial]] [[Ralsius Paldora|defector]] at [[Takodana Castle|Maz's castle]] to get information that would help in the [[liberation of Kashyyyk]] to twenty-nine [[Standard year|years]] before the [[Hosnian Cataclysm|Starkiller Incident]], which ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]'' dates to [[34 ABY]]. Therefore, the meeting and the resulting skirmish took place in [[5 ABY]]. As the destruction of an [[abandoned weapons depot]] took place between Solo's meeting with the Imperial defector, and the [[Battle of Jakku]], which ''Star Wars: Galactic Atlas'' dates to 5 ABY, Missions 7-9 must also fall in 5 ABY.</ref> ||style="background-color: #C3D69B; text-align: center;" | VG ||''[[Star Wars Battlefront II]]'' Campaign: Mission 7: General Distress

|data-sort-value=5 |During or after [[5 ABY]]<ref name="TreeofLife">"The Tree of Life" takes place after [[Lumpawaroo]] was freed in ''[[Aftermath: Empire's End]]''. ''Aftermath: Empire's End'' features the [[Battle of Jakku]], which ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]'' dates to [[5 ABY]]. Therefore, the events of "The Tree of Life" must take place during or after 5 ABY.</ref> ||style="background-color: #C6D9F0; text-align: center;" | SS ||"[[The Tree of Life]]" †

|data-sort-value=7 |[[7 ABY]]<ref name="Last Shot">''[[Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary]]'' dates [[Landonis Balthazar Calrissian|Lando Calrissian]] and [[Han Solo]]'s pursuit of [[Fyzen Gor]], as seen in ''Last Shot'', to twenty-seven [[Standard year|years]] before the [[Hosnian Cataclysm]]. ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]'' dates the Hosnian Cataclysm to [[34 ABY]], meaning that the events of ''Last Shot'' took place in [[7 ABY]].</ref> ||style="background-color: #8DB3E2; text-align: center;" | N ||''[[Last Shot]]''

|| 2018-04-17
|- class="junior"
|data-sort-value=9 |[[9 ABY]]<ref name="Hunters">''[[Hunters: Battle for the Arena]]'' takes place after the fall of the [[Galactic Empire]], which ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]'' dates to [[5 ABY]]. In the story, [[Rieve]] is 20 years old, but in a flashback, which takes place during the [[Imperial Era]], she is 16 years old. So the novel can not take place more than four years after the Fall of the Empire. As it also takes place after [[Aran Tal]] joined the [[Hunters of the Outer Rim]], which ''[[Star Wars: Timelines]]'' dates to [[9 ABY]], the book must be set in that year.</ref> ||style="background-color: #FAC08F; text-align: center;" | JR ||''[[Hunters: Battle for the Arena]]'' †

|data-sort-value=18 |c. [[18 ABY]]<ref name="Free Fall">''[[Poe Dameron: Free Fall]]'' takes place during the time in which [[Poe Dameron]] joins the [[Spice Runners of Kijimi]]. ''[[Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary]]'' states that Dameron joined the Spice Runners sixteen [[Standard year|years]] before the [[Hosnian Cataclysm]], which is dated to [[34 ABY]] by ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]''. Therefore, Dameron joined the Spice Runners in [[18 ABY]], and the novel must be set around that year.</ref> ||style="background-color: #8DB3E2; text-align: center;" | N ||''[[Poe Dameron: Free Fall]]'' †

|data-sort-value=25 |[[25 ABY]]<ref name="Scorched">''[[The Star Wars Book]]'' establishes that events of the novel ''[[Bloodline]]'' occur 28 [[Standard year|years]] after those of the film [[Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope|''Star Wars'': Episode IV ''A New Hope'']], which ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]'' dates to the year [[0 ABY]]; therefore, ''Bloodline'' takes place in [[28 ABY]]. In ''Bloodline'', [[Greer Sonnel]] states that she received her [[bloodburn]] diagnosis three years prior, and the short story "[[Scorched]]" is set when Sonnel is symptomatic but not yet diagnosed; this places "Scorched" in [[25 ABY]].</ref> ||style="background-color: #C6D9F0; text-align: center;" | SS ||"[[Scorched]]"

|data-sort-value=31 |c. [[31 ABY]]<ref name="Force Collector">In ''[[Force Collector]]'', [[Dok-Ondar]] has the [[Limb|arm]] of [[C-3PO]], which [[Gender|he]] lost during the [[mission to Taul]]. ''[[Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary]]'' states that [[Poe Dameron]] joined the [[Resistance]] three [[Standard year|years]] before the [[Hosnian Cataclysm|Starkiller Incident]], which ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]'' dates to [[34 ABY]]. Therefore, Dameron joined the Resistance in [[31 ABY]]. As Dameron is a member of the [[Resistance]] at the [[time]] of the mission to [[Taul]], it must take place during or after 31 ABY, and therefore the events of ''Force Collector'' must take place around the same time frame.</ref>||style="background-color: #8DB3E2; text-align: center;" | N ||''[[Force Collector]]'' †

|- class="short"
|data-sort-value=34|[[34 ABY]]<ref name="TPW Date">The [[Del Rey]] ''[[Star Wars]]'' timeline places "The Perfect Weapon" in between [[Canto Bight (novella collection)|''Canto Bight'']] and [[Star Wars: Episode VII The Force Awakens|''Star Wars'': Episode VII ''The Force Awakens'']]. {{SW|url=news/4-reasons-canto-bight-is-an-essential-read|text=4 Reasons ''Canto Bight'' Is an Essential Read}} states that ''Canto Bight'' takes place a few [[Standard day|days]] prior to [[Star Wars: Episode VIII The Last Jedi|''Star Wars'': Episode VIII ''The Last Jedi'']], which ''[[Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary]]'' places in the same year as the ''Star Wars'': Episode VII ''The Force Awakens''. ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]'' dates ''Star Wars'': Episode VII ''The Force Awakens'' to [[34 ABY]], meaning that both ''Star Wars'': Episode VIII ''The Last Jedi'', ''Star Wars'': Episode VII ''The Force Awakens'', and ''Canto Bight'' take place in the same year. Because "The Perfect Weapon" takes place in between ''Canto Bight'' and ''Star Wars'': Episode VII ''The Force Awakens'', it must also take place in 34 [['ABY-BBY' dating system|ABY]].</ref> ||style="background-color: #C6D9F0; text-align: center;" | SS ||"[[The Perfect Weapon]]" †
||[[Delilah S. Dawson]]

|data-sort-value=34 |[[34 ABY]]<ref name="Episode VIII">{{Film|VIII}} begins immediately after [[Star Wars: Episode VII The Force Awakens|''Star Wars'': Episode VII ''The Force Awakens'']], which ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]'' dates to [[34 ABY]]. ''[[The Star Wars Book]]'' dates the events of ''The Last Jedi'' to 34 [[Standard year|years]] after the end of [[Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope|''Star Wars'': Episode IV ''A New Hope'']], which ''Star Wars: Galactic Atlas'' dates to [[0 ABY]]. Therefore, the film and concurrent stories are set in 34 ABY.</ref> ||style="background-color: #92CDDC; text-align: center;" | F ||[[Star Wars: Episode VIII The Last Jedi|''Star Wars'': Episode VIII ''The Last Jedi'']]

|data-sort-value=34 |Between [[34 ABY]] and [[35 ABY]]<ref name="TMA/Breakout date dote">''[[Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary]]'' places the events of "[[Station to Station]]" shortly after the [[Battle of Starkiller Base]], which ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]'' dates to [[34 ABY]]. "[[The Missing Agent]]" and "[[Breakout]]," take place after "Station to Station" and before [[Star Wars: Episode IX The Rise of Skywalker|''Star Wars'': Episode IX ''The Rise of Skywalker'']]. ''Galactic Atlas'' dates the events of [[Star Wars: Episode VII The Force Awakens|''Star Wars'': Episode VII ''The Force Awakens'']] to 34 [['ABY-BBY' dating system|ABY]] and ''The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary'' places the events of [[Star Wars: Episode IX The Rise of Skywalker|''Star Wars'': Episode IX ''The Rise of Skywalker'']] one [[Standard year|year]] later. Therefore, the events of "The Missing Agent" and "Breakout" must take place between 34 ABY and 35 ABY.</ref> ||style="background-color: #B7DDE8; text-align: center;" | TV ||[[The Missing Agent|''Star Wars Resistance'': Season 2: Episode 12: "The Missing Agent"]] †
||[[Brandon Auman]]
